Introduction

Base URL: http://127.0.0.1:9000/

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Dietician AssignDiet

APIs for Dietician to assign diet to user

Assign Diet

This API is used to assign diet to user

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/dietician/diet/assign" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"user_id\": 13,
    \"diet\": \"[\\\"dolores\\\",\\\"aliquam\\\"]\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/dietician/diet/assign"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "user_id": 13,
    "diet": "[\"dolores\",\"aliquam\"]"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request   

POST api/v1/dietician/diet/assign

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

user_id   integer   

Example: 13

diet   string   

Must be a valid JSON string. Example: ["dolores","aliquam"]

Dietician Auth

APIs for user authentication/registration All auth related APIs are here

Login

This endpoint is used to authenticate dietician by token . if dietician is not found in database it will return error

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/dietician/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"muller.emmy@example.org\",
    \"password\": \"ducimus\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/dietician/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "muller.emmy@example.org",
    "password": "ducimus"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request   

POST api/v1/dietician/login

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

email   string   

Must be a valid email address. Example: muller.emmy@example.org

password   string   

Example: ducimus

Dietician Basic

@authenticated

Dietician Profile

This endpoint is used to get dietician profile

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/dietician" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/dietician"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Update Dietician Profile

This endpoint is used to update dietician profile

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/dietician/update" \
    --header "Content-Type: multipart/form-data" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --form "name=gzgvmwhoykob" \
    --form "phone=ocgvgtchxm" \
    --form "address=cvzdfqqofwcuqvyndy" \
    --form "image=@C:\Users\7854\AppData\Local\Temp\php47F5.tmp" 
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/dietician/update"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('name', 'gzgvmwhoykob');
body.append('phone', 'ocgvgtchxm');
body.append('address', 'cvzdfqqofwcuqvyndy');
body.append('image', document.querySelector('input[name="image"]').files[0]);

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request   

POST api/v1/dietician/update

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: multipart/form-data

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

name   string   

Must not be greater than 255 characters. Example: gzgvmwhoykob

image   file  optional  

Must be an image. Must not be greater than 512 kilobytes. Example: C:\Users\7854\AppData\Local\Temp\php47F5.tmp

phone   string   

Must be 10 characters. Example: ocgvgtchxm

address   string   

Must not be greater than 3000 characters. Example: cvzdfqqofwcuqvyndy

Get Templates

This endpoint is used to get templates You can also get single template by id if id is not provided, all templates will be returned if id is provided, single template will be returned with its recipes

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/dietician/templates/et" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/dietician/templates/et"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

User Auth

APIs for user authentication/registration All auth related APIs are here

Login

This endpoint is used to authenticate user by token or register new user if user is not found in database it will create new user and return it with token if user is found in database it will return old user with new token

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/user/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"token\": \"<<json web token>>\",
    \"device_id\": \"1e6c1d3c2f5b4f6d8c3e5a7b9c6d8f5e\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/user/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "token": "<<json web token>>",
    "device_id": "1e6c1d3c2f5b4f6d8c3e5a7b9c6d8f5e"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

User Chat

APIs for User Chat

Get Active Chat

requires authentication

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/user/chat/active" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/user/chat/active"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Send Message

requires authentication

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/user/chat/send-message" \
    --header "Content-Type: multipart/form-data" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --form "message=upcobukjtnftl" \
    --form "media[]=@C:\Users\7854\AppData\Local\Temp\php46AC.tmp" 
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/user/chat/send-message"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('message', 'upcobukjtnftl');
body.append('media[]', document.querySelector('input[name="media[]"]').files[0]);

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());

User Diet

APIs for User to get diet

Get Diet

This API is used to get diet for user if days is not provided then it will return diet for next 7 days

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/user/diet" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"days\": 13
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/user/diet"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "days": 13
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

User Like

APIs for User To Like/Unlike

Toggle Like Blog

This endpoint is used to like/unlike a blog

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/user/like/toggle/blog" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"blog_id\": 1
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:9000/api/v1/user/like/toggle/blog"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "blog_id": 1
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):


{
    "status": "success",
    "message": "You have successfully liked/un-liked {blog_title}"
}
